The huge construction could hold up to 50,000 spectators who could access the arena through 8 doors. After the fall of the Roman Empire, the Colosseum was abandoned for centuries until it became a fortress during the Middle Ages. The structure was later looted of its precious marble from the Roman nobility.<br /><br />Legend has it that by throwing a coin into the Trevi Fountain you will have the certainty of returning one day to Rome. This legend and the magnificent architectural beauty, make this fountain one of the most popular and photographed monuments of Rome. Designed by Nicola Salvi in the 18th century, it became famous thanks to Federico Fellini, author of the film "La dolce vita". At the center of the fountain stands Neptune the God of the sea that brings back to the mythology of ancient Rome.
